 The BJP government, which came to power in May 2014, had said in the election manifesto to bring back black money and curb it
 sarkaar banate hi modi ne kai kade kadam uthaae
 Surgical strike on black money
 
 
 modi sarkaar ke 7 kade kadam1- blike mani par SIT kaa gathansatta main aane ke saath hi modi sarkaar ne supreme court ke aadesh par kaale dhan ke khilaaf esaiti kaa gathan karne kaa faisla kiya

 2- jan dhan yojanapradhanmantri narendra modi ne 28 agast, 2014 ko pradhanmantri jan dhan yojana kaa shubharambh kiya tha
 Modi had shown personal interest in the scheme
 jin logon ke bank main kinhi vajahon se khate nahin khul pate the, unke khate khul gaye
 Due to which the record 1 across the country on the first day

 25 by this time under the scheme
 45 karod logon ke back acount khul gaye hai

 4- Overseas Black Money and Imposition of Tax Act, 2015 To curb Indian black money abroad, the Modi Government passed the Black Money and Imposition of Tax Act, 2015 in Parliament
 iske saath hi sarkaar ne kalaadhan kanoon ke tahat videsh se hone vaali aay or sampatti kaa moolyankan ke niyamon ko lagu kar diya
 This rule came into force from July 1, 2015
 isamen videshi sampattiyon or aay kaa khulaasa nahin karne par sakht sajaa kaa praavdhaan kiya gaya he
 Through this, concealment of income from foreign assets and tax evasion can be punishable by 10 years
 iske alaava 300 pratishat jurmaana bhi lagaaya jayega
 At the same time, after the new law, the guilty will not be allowed to go to the Settlement Commission
 aghoshit videshi sampatti se hone vaali aay par adhiktam dar se tex lagegaa or koi chhot yaa katautee agar lagu he, to nahin milegi
 5- Income Declaration Scheme, 2016 Modi government implemented IDS Income Declaration Scheme from June 1, 2016 to curb black money
 yah skim 30 sitambar tak jari rahaa
 This scheme was created to bring out black money
 is skim ke tahat kaale dhan kaa khulaasa karne vaale ko 45 fisadi tex dena tha
 There was a facility to pay this tax in installments
 nagdi main bhi tex jamaa kiya ja saktaa tha
 Under this, no action was taken against those who declared black money
 kaala dhan ghoshit karne waalon kaa naam puri tarah se gupt rakhaa gaya
 6 - Reduction of black money in real estate The government also changed the Income Tax Act to curb black money in real estate
 is act ke section 269SS or 269T ke praavdhaan main sanshodhan kiya gaya
 Under this, cash transactions of more than 20 thousand were banned in real estate
 ise zyada len-dein par 20 fisadi jurmaana lagaaya gaya
 It was made compulsory to provide PAN for the purchase and sale of property of more than 1 lakh
 7- benami len-dein (pratibandh) sanshodhankale dhan par ankush lagane ke benami len-dein (pratibandh) sanshodhan bill ko sansad main paas kiya gaya
 It entered into force on 1 November 2016
 iske jariye real estate or sone kii kharidari main benami rup se ho rahe len-dein par lagaam lagaai jaaegi
 The bill provides for imprisonment of black money abroad for ten years and a fine of ninety percent
 yah jurmaana us par lagane vaale tees pratishat kar ke atirikt hoga
 The new law also provides that hiding property information in filing returns will result in a sentence of up to seven years

[endif] congress adhyaksharahul gandhi apane videshi daure par bhartiya janata party or rashtriya swayamsevak sangh (RSS) par jamkar hamalaa bolaa
 Now the Sangh has retaliated on Rahul's allegations
 aresaiske pravaktaa rajeev tuli ne ajtak se baat karte hue kaha ki rahul gandhi ko din-raat RSS ke sapane aate hai, unhen hamaari chintaa naa karte hue apni party kii chintaa kerani chahie
 Rajiv Tuli said that because Rahul dreams of RSS, his party came down to 44
 kahin aisa naa ho ki agle chunaav main unki siten or bhi kam ho jaaen
 He said that RSS was formed in 1925, Rashtra Sevika Samiti was formed in 1936
 isaki desh main 5000 se adhikshakhalagati hai, jo desh main mahilaon ke vikaas main kaam karti he
 Please tell that Rahul said that you will never get to see a woman in the RSS
 ise padhein
 
 congress ne jari kiya rahul kaa berlin vaala bhaashan, kaha- BJP-RSS desh ko baant raheitna hi nahin unhone kaha ki main rahul gandhi ke salaahkaaron se kahana chahta hum ki rahul gandhi ko ek baar aresas kii shakha main aana chahie or ek do saal sangh main bitaane chahie, usko baad unako desh kii aatma or desh kii samskruti kaa gyaan ho jaayegaa
 There have been natural disasters in Kerala where the Sangh is working shoulder to shoulder with the army
 lekin rahul gandhi germany main sangh ke sapane dekh rahe hai unhen badnaam kar rahe hai
 i think Sangh is beyond comprehension for Rahul Gandhi
 unhone kaha ki rahul gandhi ko pranab mukherjee se siikhnaa chahie jinhen desh kii samskruti or desh ke bare main gyaan he
 Sangh spokesperson said that Rahul Gandhi cannot understand the country and the Sangh for the next two to three births, so he must come to the Sangh branch once if even after that he does not understand the country and the Sangh, then of course leave 
 lekin mujhe yakeen he rahul gandhi ek baar sangh kii shakha main aa jaaen, phir vah sangh chhodkar nahin jaaenge
 The second match of the five-match Test series between Team India and England will be played at the historic ground of Lord's
 toss se pehle hi landan main halki barish ho rahi he, jiske kaaran toss main deree hui he
 In this Test match, former India captain Sourav Ganguly has advised Virat Kohli to feed Ashwin as well as Kuldeep Yadav
 ganguli ne bharat ko lords test main do spinners ke saath utarane kii salaah di he
 In a column written in the Times of India, Ganguly said that England had given a chance to their young player Ol Pope, a well-thought-out strategy of English selectors, betting on them to counter an off-spin attack
 lords main phiseddi england, 7 saal main ek baar bhi asian team ko haraa nahin piganguli ke mutabik aise main bharat ko apane duusare spinners ko team main mauka dena chahie
 Lord's history has been that the ball spins here
 jahaan tak main sochataa hum, to iske liye kuldeep yadav ek behatar chois honge
 Ganguly said that India should not compromise with its 5-spoke option under any circumstances
 lords main apane debyue match main shatak jadne vaale saurav ganguli ne team siries main 1-0 se pichad chuki team india ke liye kaha ki lords test main team ko damakham dikhaanaa hoga
 England would not like to give India a chance here very easily
 IND vs ENG aalochak mat bano, samasya takneekee nahin maansik he: kohliunhone kaha, 'agar bharat kii batting yahaan chali, to vah match main jeet darj kar saktaa he or ek baar phir flop hue, to mehmaan team ke liye chijen badalane main der nahin lagegi
 Ganguly also praised Ravichandran Ashwin, who is impressed with his performance
 unhone kaha, 'bharat ke liye uski gendbaaji positive cheez rahi, sabhi bolers ne acha kaam kiya, khaastaur se aswin ne
 He showed great variety in his bowling and now he will be a challenge for the opposition team in the rest of the series
 ' Sony TV show 'power Couple' is being launched in Goa
 is sho main chote parde ke kai bade actor najar aaenge
 Pratyusha Banerjee and many others including Rahul Raj Singh, Mehak Chahal and Ashmit Patel, Karishma Tanna and Upen Patel, Sanjeeda Sheikh and Aamir Ali, Shilpa Sakalani and Apoorva Agnihotri, Mugdha Godse and Rahul Dev, Delnaz Irani and Percy Karkaria, Saeeda Jafri and Naved Jafri Artists will be seen
 yah sho soni televijan par shanivaar-ravivaar raat 8 baje dikhaaya jayega
 The entire shooting of this show will be done in Goa
 soni antertenment televijan ke aagaamisho 'power kapal' main arbaj ko apni patni malaika arodaake saath mejabani karte dekha jayega
 'power Couple' will air on television from December 12
 khap netaaon ne supreme court ke nirdeshon kaa paalan karte hue 14 janvari ko apane pratinidhiyon ko nyaayalay bhejne kaa faisla kiya he
 Along with this, the Khapas have said that love marriage and marriage in the same gotra are not acceptable at any cost
 85 gaanv kii panchayaton ne milakar ye faisla kiya he
 The Supreme Court had given instructions that on 4 January, the Supreme Court sent a notice to the Central Government regarding the protection of women from the absurd orders of Khap Panchayats
 notice main kaha gaya tha ki khap panchayat par sarkaar kadi najar banaae rakhe
 Along with this, the Supreme Court had also directed the Khap representatives to appear in the court on 14 January
 court kaa kahana tha ki wo khap panchayat kaa paksh bhi sunanaa chaahate hai
 Apart from this, the IG (crime) of Jind and Baghpat districts of Haryana was also summoned by the Supreme Court

 mishrit yugal varg ke pehle quarter final main indonesia ke tontovi ahamed or liliana naastir kii sheersh variya jodi korea ke baeke choel shin or ye naa jang kii jodi ko 21-18, 21-16 se haraakar antim-4 main pahunchi
 In the mixed doubles, Korea's Sung Hyun Ko and Ha Na Kim defeated seventh seeded pair of Indonesia's Fran Kurniawan and Shendi Irawati 19-21, 21-19, 21-12
 isi varg ke tisare quarter final match main england ke kris adcock or gabriel white kii jodi ne thailand kii sudaket pi
 And Saralee T
 kii jodi ko 19-21, 21-11, 21-15 se haraaya

 in donon ke bich yah paanchavin bhidnt hogi
 Shank has won four times till now
 purush ekal main pranoy ko vishwa ke sarvocch variyata praapt thailand ke lee chong vei ne 21-14, 21-19 se haraaya
 The match proved to be a great experience for Prannoy
 pranoy ne duusare game main ek samay 14-18 kii badhat le lee thi lekin uske baad vah apni hi galatiyon kaa shikaar hue
 By the way, Prannoy did a great job overall and managed to push Wei to the backfoot on several occasions
 purush ekal varg main pranit ko toornament ke chathe variya japani khilaadi kenchi taago se 17-21, 21-19, 11-21 se haar mili
 Praneeth lost this match in one hour and two minutes
 taago semifinal main pavaar se bhidenge

 yah match 30 minute chalaa

 donon do-do baar jite hai

 yah match 58 minute chalaa

 purush yugal ke antim-8 daur ke mukaable main china ke jiyolong liyu or jihan kyuu kii aathvin variya jodi ne denmark ke mathais boe or carsten mogensen kii sheersh variya jodi ko 21-19, 21-19 se haraaya

 The International Monetary Fund (IMF) issued a report on Wednesday strongly condemning the Greece agreement in the eurozone

 pradhanmantri sipraas ke liye kadi chunautigris kii media main trend kar rahi khabaron ke mutabik desh kii sattarudh left party bill ke khilaaf khadaa hoga or vah belout package ke bajaae waapas gharelu mudra dirham kii ore lautne kii baat rakhega

 uttar pradesh ke lakhanu main rahane vaale chanaa laal ko ab koi ummid nahin
 They have given up
 unhen koi ummid nahin ki unka vikrut cheharaa kabhi thik ho paaegaa
 He has given up hope that a 4 kg 'trunk' made on his face will ever be operated
 unhone sweekaar liya he ki ab taumr unhen dard ke saath hi rahanaa hoga
 Lal, 35 years old, lives in a village on the outskirts of Lucknow
 chehre se lekar chaati tak nikle tumor kii vajah se ve na to thik se kha pate hai or na hi bol pate hai
 They do not see the mirror and live alone
 unki do bhatijiyaan unka dhyaan rakhti hai

 pehle unka cheharaa halkaa sa vikrut tha, lekin dhire-dhire vah hathi kii sound ke aakaar jaisaa ho gaya
 He tried to get the operation done 10 years ago, but he got so much blood that he somehow survived
 tab unhen doctoron ne hidaayat di ki agar wo jinda rahanaa chaahate hai to phir kabhi oparation na karaaen
 Lal is the youngest of his eight siblings
 or unki do bhatijiyaan rojaanaa ke kaamon main unki madad karti hai
 He says, 'I am ugly
 mujhe khud ko shishe main dekhnaa bhi pasand nahin
 i also don't like anyone seeing me
 main oparation karana chahta hum, lekin mujhe thik hone kii koi ummid nahin
 i was dead at the time of operation last time
 isliye mujhe nahin lagata ki is chehre kaa kuch ho saktaa he'
 When Lal was younger, he had a small scar on his face, but his parents were very poor and there was no hospital nearby
 aath saal kii umr tak unhen kisi doctor ko nahin dikhaaya gaya
 Recalling the old days, Lal says, "when the children used to run away after seeing me, i started feeling that there was something wrong in my face
 mujhe yaad he ki main apni maa ke paas jaakar royaa tha or unhone mujhase sidhe-sidhe kaha ki tumhaara cheharaa bhayanak he
 Since then i have never asked any child to play with me
 usee laal ke swargeey mata-pita unhen doctor ke paas le gaye, lekin ilaaj ke liye 15,000 rupee kii jarurat thi
 This amount was too big for the family and they came back home
 us vakt ek sarkas ne unke gharavaalon se unhen unke saath bhejne ke liye kaha or badale main paison kii peshkash kii, lekin unhone manaa kar diya
 When Lal was 25 years old, the family members arranged for the money and took him to the doctor
 oparation ke dauraan mukhya rakt nalee katate hi unka bahut khun nikalne laga
 After this, the doctors told their family members that if you want to keep your son alive then do not get his operation done again
 laal kaa tumor ab itnaa bad gaya ki unke baayen aankh kii roshan chali gai he or wo baayen kaan se sun bhi nahin pate hai
 They say, 'I can't even chew anything because my jaws are also sunken and my teeth can't do their job
 main jaananaa chahta hum ki aakhir raseele seb kaa swaad kaisaa hota he'
 Reds sometimes wage
 lekin is tarah ke shareerik kaam se unhen behad dard hota he

 agar maalik ne sun liya to wo mujhe kaam nahin degaa'
 Lal lives alone, but his niece Suman takes care of him
 suman ke mutabik, 'jab main apane chachaa ko akelaa dekhati hum to mujhe bahut bura lagata he
 i want them to live like other people too
 jab main choti thi to unke chehre ko dekhakar dar jaaya karti thi
 But now i get used to it
 vah bahut hi mridubhashi or achche insaan hai
 i have never seen him angry
 ham unke liye patni dhundne kii koshish kar rahe hai, lekin unki haalat dekhakar koi aage nahin badhata
 i want his future wife to love him a lot '
 vahiin, chanaa laal ko koi ummid nahin

 jab laal ghar se baahar jate hai to log unhen bhagwaan ganesh kaa avatar maanane lagate hai

 unhen lagata he ki main bhagwaan hum
 But they make me angry because i am not God
 agar main bhagwaan hota to main itani takalif main nahin hota'
 Sometimes being more beautiful becomes a hindrance
 shashi kapur agar thode kam khubasurat, thode kam aakarshak hote to hindi cinema kii diggaj shakhsiyaton main kab ke shumaar ho gaye hote
 The filmmaker wanted to capitalize on his 'look' and introduced him as a romantic star
 lekin unke 77wein janmdin ke kuch din baad hi bhartiya cinema main yogadan ke liye unhen 2014 kaa dada sahib phalke puraskaar die jane kaa elaan shaayad is ninsaphi ko kuch kam kar de
 This will inspire film critics and historians to reevaluate not only his evergreen performances but also a risk-taking filmmaker and his contribution to theater
 shashi kapur film star nahin bananaa chaahate the
 At the age of 15 he went to his father Prithviraj Kapoor's Prithvi Theater for Rs 75
 masik par kaam karne lage
 He continued to work there until the theater closed in 1960
 ve theatre ke har fan main maahir hona chaahate the
 From acting to the lighting of the stage, the decor and the entire management, they wanted everyone to take care
 ve cinema ke takneekee pahaluon ko jaanane ko utsuk the or prithvi theatre se lekar bade bhai raaj kapur ke aar
 K
 studio ke bich jhulate rahete
 Raj Kapoor sent him to study lighting at the top of the studio and advised, "feel the heat
" "unhen apane donon bade bhaaiyon se zyada hi garmi kaa ehsaas karnaa padaa
 Both were tough in terms of work
 unhen raaj or shammi kapur kii chodi gai bhoomikaayen bhi nibhaani padin
 They often had to go to extras in the drama troupe of Prithvi Theater as an extra
 jab ve sahaayak stage manjar bana die gaye to unhen kai baar trek ke upar baithkar manch kii saaj-sajja or kapadon kii rakhwali kerani padati thi
 He also went on to star as a child when he played Raj Kapoor's Chhutpan in Aag (1948) and Awara (1951)
 dabl shift unke shuruaati kariyar kaa hissaa tha
 He would take turns in Prithvi Theater and Shakespeareana
 shakespraana bhi ghumantu theatre company thi, jise jenifer candal ke pita jyafri candal chalaate the
 Jennifer later became his wife
 18 varsh kii umr main shashi kapur kii mulaakaat jenifer se hui thi
 On the one hand he was active in contemporary Hindi theater of that time (shakuntala is an exception) and on the other hand in Shakespeare's plays
 unhone marchent of venice main gratiyano or othelo main kassiyo kii bhoomika nibhaai
 He remained with Shakespeareana until 1963
 shaayad vahiin unke abhinay main nikhaar aayaa

 unhone mujhe penang restaraan kaa kissa bataaya tha jab unhone 'ek bouvel rice' mangaaye

 jyafri apni bear chhodkar aae or kaha, "bawel nahin bevakoof, ball
 "that is how the two started talking
 20 varsh kii umr main shashi kapur kii shaadi hui or apane pehle bachche kunal ke janm ke samay unki umr 21 varsh thi
 Concerned with this, he began to work in Hindi films with reluctance
 haalanki 1961 main chaar deewari se shuru hokar yash chopra nirdeshit dharmaputra tak, unki shuruaati kuch filmein box offis par naakaam raheen
 After five years, this phase of flops broke and his Jab Jab Phool Khile (1965) was successful, which was the heroine Nanda
 yah jodi saat filmon tak bani rahi
 Perhaps Raj Kapoor had asked Nanda to 'take care' of his younger brother
 1960 ke dashak ke aakhri varshon main unki kai romantic kamedi filmein hit huin

 1970 ke dashak main unka jalawaa rahaa or amitabh bachchan ke saath unki diwaar (1975), kabhi-kabhi (1976), trishul (1978) or suhaag (1979) jaisi safal filmein ain
 The pair continued to give successful films like Silsila (1981) and Namak Halal (1982) even in the early 1990s
 industry main to yah galat majaak aam ho gaya tha ki shashi kapur bachchan kii pasandida heroin hai
 If Shashi Kapoor had not played a great character in the wall, she would not have become a 'milestone' in Hindi cinema
 apni bhoomika ko sanyat rakh unhone parade par bigdel bhai amitabh kii atinaatakeey bhoomika ko santulit bana diya
 His acting abilities blossom in films in which he evokes intricacies of human tendency
 khaskar un do filmon main jinke nirmaataa ve khud or nirdeshak shyaam benegal the
 In passion, they express love to the extent of insanity, while in the Mahabharata, they play the role of Karna of modern times
 unhone uski pidaa, hataasha or chaturaai kaa bakhubi pradarshan kiya he
 Shashi Kapoor is perhaps the first real international star of Indian cinema
 sirf sabu dastagir ko iskaa apwaad kaha ja saktaa he jo hollywood main mughali bane the
 Shashi acted in six films of merchant-ivory
 shuruyaat 1963 main houseolder se hui
 Two years later, shakespeare-walla arrived
 1970 main bombai toki or 1982 main hit and dust
 Heat and Dust brought him international fame
 usamen ve romani par chaalaak nawab kii bhoomika main hai
 shakespeare-wala failed commercially but was caught by international directors
 preti poli (1967) main ve hele mills ke saath romantic kirdaar main utre, jiske nirdeshak auskar puraskaar praapt gaai green the
 American director Conard Rooks took him to Siddharth in 1972
 america nirdeshak jex iveri ne mujhase kaha tha ki shashi kapur bharat main kairi grant jaise abhinayta ho sakate the, basharte unhen achche nirdeshak milte
 He also believed that he was adept at elevating the dark side of humans
 bombai toki par charchaa main unhone kaha, "sabakaa syah paksh hota he or shashi ise ubhaarne main sakasham hai
 "international directors elevate his dark side, be it the crafty gentleman in The Deceiver (1988) who cheats or the mean Pakistani businessman in Stephen Farriers' Sammy and Rosie Get Led (1987), based on Hanif Qureshi's screenplay
 divangat film sameekshak polin kel ne unki kaaphi tarif kii thi
 Among his other international roles are the character of New York's Bollywood actor undergoing bad times in Tony Garber's Side Streets (1998) and the angel Jibral in Jamil Dehalvi's Jinnah (1998)
 unhone enbisi kii tivi shrunkhlaa gulivers travels main bhi bhoomika nibhaai thi
 Shashi Kapoor's most memorable role is as a producer
 baaki logon ke ulat, ve apni banaai chah filmon ke financer bhi the
 This is typical of the Kapoor family
 raaj kapur ne film banane ke liye apni patni ke jevar bech die to chote bhai ne 36 chaurangi len banane ke liye mumbai ke upnagar panwel kii apni 18 acre jameen bech di thi

 ab ve kamjor or wheelchair par hai
